Strategic Interpretation

Aruangos Down Rebels won because their adaptive highland forest approach translated into an early and midgame treasury edge, which mattered more than the region race on a thirty-seven-region ring. While Rnutuan Gate Rebels and later Aruangos Down Rebels led in regions at different points, neither converted those territorial swings into lasting economic separation, which left the board open but the score decided by income. Veneunar Field Rebels finished with 6 regions and 204 treasury, so their position was too small economically to overcome the winner’s 283 treasury and 9 regions.
The closest challenger was Veneunar Field Rebels (Adaptive Coast) at 204 treasury and 6 regions.

Victor's History

The Aruangos Down Rebels prevailed not by spectacle, but by disciplined conversion of position into treasury, and that edge proved decisive from the early and mid phases onward. Their Adaptive Highland Forest habits, shaped by geography, gave them a coherent method that held even after their regions peaked and then settled at 9 by the end. Others could lead in regions for stretches, as Rnutuan Gate Rebels did early and midgame, but such advantages did not endure against a faction that managed its resources with greater efficiency. In the end, the winning margin belonged to steadier judgment and superior economic conversion, not to temporary territorial display.
